| 2:37:42| in this broadband build-out.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-210629?start=9462)|
| 2:37:44| During the beginning of the pandemic, KUV temporarily suspended utility disconnections| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-210629?start=9464)|
| 2:37:49| and did so for longer than most other utilities in the TVA footprint, which is really commendable.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-210629?start=9469)|
| 2:37:54| KUV also worked very hard with NOx, CAC, and other groups to coordinate utility bill support| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-210629?start=9474)|
| 2:37:59| for households in need while disconnections had been suspended.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-210629?start=9479)|
| 2:38:04| But in spite of these best efforts, 3,000 households were disconnected from their utility| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-210629?start=9484)|
| 2:38:08| services between October of 2020, when KUV resumed their shutoffs, and February of 2021.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-210629?start=9488)|
| 2:38:15| Meanwhile, more than 16,000 customers owed utility bill debt to KUV at the time disconnections| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-210629?start=9495)|
| 2:38:21| were resumed in October.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-210629?start=9501)|
| 2:38:24| The NOxville Water and Energy for All campaign, which involves organizations like One NOx| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-210629?start=9504)|
| 2:38:28| Legacy, Three Cubed, NOxville Service Industry United, and Appalachian Voices, have conducted| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-210629?start=9508)|
| 2:38:34| research on the impacts of utility bill debt and utility disconnections on KUV customers| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-210629?start=9514)|
| 2:38:40| using data that was shared with us by KUV.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-210629?start=9520)|
| 2:38:44| Through this research, we found it is likely that all KUV customers at 150 percent of the| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-210629?start=9524)|
| 2:38:49| federal poverty line have utility bills that are higher than 10 percent of their income,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-210629?start=9529)|
| 2:38:53| which is considered unaffordable by experts across the country.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-210629?start=9533)|
| 2:38:57| Perhaps more importantly, we found that communities of color are 200 percent more likely to be| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-210629?start=9537)|
| 2:39:02| disconnected from their utilities than white neighborhoods served by KUV.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-210629?start=9542)|
| 2:39:07| And communities of color also owe twice as much utility bill debt, illustrating a clear| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-210629?start=9547)|
| 2:39:12| racial disparity and need for utility justice at KUV.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-210629?start=9552)|
| 2:39:17| We're really grateful to KUV for sharing this data with us and for joining us in many conversations| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-210629?start=9557)|
| 2:39:22| about this issue.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-210629?start=9562)|
| 2:39:24| But it's also important to point out that this is the first time that research to identify| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-210629?start=9564)|
| 2:39:28| the impacts of utility burden and utility disconnections on different demographics has| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-210629?start=9568)|
| 2:39:33| been conducted for the KUV service area.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-210629?start=9573)|
| 2:39:37| One solution that could address the serious problem of utility bill unaffordability at| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-210629?start=9577)|
| 2:39:41| KUV is a percentage of income payment plan, or a PIP.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-210629?start=9581)|
| 2:39:45| PIPs are designed to limit utility bills to an affordable level of less than 10 percent| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-210629?start=9585)|
| 2:39:50| of income for low-income customers.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-210629?start=9590)|
| 2:39:52| They've been implemented successfully at utilities across the country.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/city-council-r-265-210629?start=9592)|
